Summer Scenery in Qingmin Garden, Donggou 158

Lotus Flowers in Full Bloom, Fragrance Carried by the Clear Breeze

Specially Prepared Distilled Water to Brew Red and Green Aromatic Tea

Since the Donggou Municipal Scenic Garden began opening day and night last week after renovating the garden and installing electric lights, the number of people going there to escape the heat has been endless every day at 2 PM. At 11:30 PM, when the ferry for the cool off trip returned to Shanghai, there were still people lingering and reluctant to leave, which shows how cool and elegant it is. This reporter went for a visit. Take the municipal ferry from the steel pier of the Bund in Nanjing Road to Donggou and disembark. Walk east along Donggou Road for about a hundred steps and you will see red and green electric lights shining brightly, which is the main gate of the garden. The words "Qingliang Garden" (Cool Garden) are attached to the gate. Entering the gate, the shadows of the trees are jagged and the green shadows are colorful, making you feel refreshed and invigorated. In the western part of the garden, there is a small stream, with winding streams. Willow trees are planted along the stream and a road is built along the stream leading to the earthen mountain. There is a pavilion on the mountain and a grassland on the side of the mountain, a green expanse. Sitting and walking is very pleasing to the eyes. In front of the grassland is a tea room, with various drinks available, and red and green famous teas are brewed with distilled water. Tourists often sit and chat, taste tea, and reminisce about the old days. In front of the room, the earth rises and falls under the mountain, surrounded by a lotus pond. A small bridge is built over the pond, with green waves and red railings, which is ancient and elegant. Moreover, the garden is full of clear breeze and the fragrance of lotus flowers, as if in a cool world, a truly winning place. After the tour, it was midnight. At 11 o'clock, I took the cool-off boat back. The sea is troubled and the heat is pressing. Why not go for a visit to breathe the cool air?

Page 13

Famous Person in Shanghai

Shao Wenbin Suddenly Assassinated 159

Shao's Operation of Flower Shows and Gambling Has Been Very Successful in Recent Years

Men in Dark Blue Silk Gowns Fired a Barrage of Shots

Shao Wenbin Dies Tragically at the Intersection of Rue Delorme

One Assailant Shot Dead by Two Detectives

Four Bystanders Wounded by Stray Bullets

At 8:45 last night, a shooting occurred on Rue Amiral Courbet in the French Concession. The victim was Shao Wenbin, a well-known figure in Shanghai. He was shot five times and died at the scene. There were five assailants. One of them fled to the gate of the residence of the late Shanghai merchant Huang Chu Jiu, 914 Avenue Edouard VII in the International Settlement (now changed to the Beijing Bookstore), and was shot and killed by Chinese Constable No. 632. Four people were wounded by stray bullets. The details are as follows:

Operating Flower Shows and Gambling 160

Shao Wenbin (nickname A'liu), a local Shanghai native, was 50 years old. He was fond of traditional music, so he learned Shen Opera (commonly known as Shanghai Opera). He first entered the Xiaoshijie, then the Xinshijie, and then the Xinxin Garden when it opened. Before he could complete his term, he stopped performing. Shao then abandoned his old profession and sought other ways out. Recently, he has been diligently operating the illegal flower shows and gambling business. His daily income is still substantial. He also has an old-fashioned carriage car for transportation and lives at 2939 in the Concession.

Investigation of Family Situation 161

Shao's elder brother, Wenrong, is 63 years old. He used to be in the shipping business and now lives at 19 Lane 4, Ronglan Fang, Route Cardinal Mercier in the French Concession. Shao and his concubine, Ms. Chen (33 years old), live with his elder brother. He also rented room 423 in the Far East Hotel on Xizang Road with his friend Huang Zhifu (nickname Monk) for entertainment. However, Shao always had lunch and dinner with his elder brother. Shao has a son named Ganlin, 18 years old, who is also living with his elder brother.

Someone Calls "Brother A'liu" 162

Yesterday, after Shao had lunch at his brother's house, he took his car at about 3 PM to Xiaoyaochi Bathhouse at the corner of Ningbo Road in East Xinjiao Street to take a bath. After chatting with his friends, it was already 8:30 in the evening. He got dressed and took his car to the Far East Hotel. After Shao got out of the car, he ordered the driver, Chen Baoli, to drive the car back to get gas and then wait at the original place. The driver obeyed the order and drove the car away. Shao saw the car driving away and was about to turn around and enter the gate of the Far East when he suddenly heard someone shout "Brother A'liu" from behind.

Barrage of Shots Fired at Shao 163

Shao turned around and looked carefully and saw two people wearing raw silk shirts and pants, whom he knew. He asked them what was the matter. The two briefly told him a few words. The three then took a rickshaw together and went south. They then turned into Route Amiral Courbet and stopped at the intersection of Rue Delorme. Shao had just gotten out of the rickshaw when three men in dark blue silk gowns suddenly came from across the street and rushed to Shao, pulled out their guns, and fired a barrage of shots at Shao. Another person went north along Hongyun Lane, crossed Avenue Edouard VII, and went to the gate of the residence of the late Shanghai merchant Huang Chu Jiu, opposite the Nanjing Grand Theater.

Assailant and Bystanders Injured 164

When Shao was attacked, there were many people cooling off by the roadside. When they saw the shooting, they blew the whistle. At the same time, Chinese Constables No. 1961 and No. 2249, who were on duty at the intersection of Avenue des Courses and Rue Dragon in the International Settlement, heard the alarm and drew their guns. They suspected it was a robbery. They saw a man rushing across the road with a gun in his hand and ordered him to stop, but he ignored them. So they fired at him. The two constables fired a total of sixteen shots. The assailant was hit by eight bullets and fell to the ground. At this time, stray bullets wounded four people: Fan Zhongyi, 37 years old, from Baoshan, a snack vendor, wounded in the left foot; Shen Chaozong, 19 years old, from Zhenjiang, wounded in the right foot; Chuan Wenhua, 25 years old, a local Shanghai native (employee of Changshou Pharmacy), wounded in the right leg; and an old woman, Dai Zhou, 69 years old, a local Shanghai native, wounded in the right foot.

Assailant Dies in Hospital 165

The injured assailant and the four people wounded by stray bullets were sent to the Renji Hospital. The thief died in the hospital due to his injuries. The other four had minor injuries and were discharged from the hospital. One was seriously injured and remained in the hospital. As for the main victim, Shao Wenbin, he had died at the scene. The police notified the Tongren Auxiliary Yuan Hall to send a hall porter to carry the body to the morgue. There were a total of five gunshot wounds on his body: one on the left and right chest, one on the back, and one on the head. Shao's white silk gown was covered in blood. At the same time, the body of the dead thief was also carried from the hospital to the morgue. The police immediately sent fingerprint personnel with equipment to the morgue to take the fingerprints of the two bodies, pending the inspection by the First Special Court today.

Fengxiang and Huian Collided; Yesterday, Ship Surveyors Were Hired to Inspect 166

Fengxiang Unloaded Cargo Yesterday; Huian Continued to Export as Usual

Responsibility Issue to be Negotiated Between the Two Parties

Taifeng Shipping Company's Fengxiang collided with Zhengji Shipping Company's Huian, which was leaving for Yantai and Andong, on the Yangjiadu waterfront the day before yesterday afternoon. Yesterday, ship surveyors were hired to inspect the damage and make a public judgment according to law. The details are as follows:

Hiring Ship Surveyors 167

After Zhengji Company's Huian was hit, the iron plates in the middle cabin were damaged. The export was stopped and the ship was sailed back to the Dong Province Railway Pier. They hired ship surveyor Engels to inspect the damage. At the same time, they sent a letter to Taifeng Company stating that the losses incurred by Huian should be fully borne by Fengxiang. They requested that personnel be sent immediately to inspect the damage to Huian.

Fengxiang Repairs 168

After Taifeng Company's Fengxiang was hit, a hole was broken in the bow and the iron plates and rivets were damaged. It was sailed to Hongsheng Pier in Pudong to unload the cargo. It also sent a reply to Zhengji Company, requesting that personnel be sent to inspect the damage to Fengxiang. It was decided that after the cargo was unloaded, it would be sailed to Gaochang Temple to anchor for repairs.

Inspection of Damage 169

At 4 PM the day before yesterday, Mr. Engels, a surveyor from the Zhengji Company, went to the Dong Province Railway pier to inspect the damage to the Huian vessel. However, due to the vessel being fully loaded with cargo, the inspection was difficult. He immediately ordered the cargo in the middle hold to be removed. He revisited the ship at 9 AM yesterday for a follow-up inspection. The results showed that the iron plates in the middle hold were damaged, but it was above the waterline and not a major problem. Zhengji Company decided that, given the cargo already loaded, they would make minor repairs to the damaged area and proceed with the export as planned, with more thorough repairs to be carried out after returning to Shanghai.

Preliminary Consultation 170

The Huian vessel set sail as scheduled last night for Yantai and Andong. The Fengxiang vessel will be repaired as soon as the cargo is unloaded. As for the issue of responsibility for the collision, the Taifeng Company and Zhengji Company began direct consultations yesterday to find a solution. As both sides have a good, amicable relationship, if a resolution cannot be reached, the matter will be submitted for legal judgment, or reported to the Navigation Administration Bureau to establish a collision dispute resolution committee.

Major Organizational Changes at the Shanghai Office of the Dalian Steamship Company 171

Transportation Concentrated in the Northeast

Development of Manchurian and Mongolian Export Goods

Shanghai Reduced to Third-Class Branch

Shanghai is an important seaport for foreign trade in China. Export goods from all ports along the Yangtze River are concentrated in Shanghai and transshipped for export. Imported goods destined for the interior also mostly transit through Shanghai. Therefore, shipping companies from all countries regard Shanghai as the central hub of the Far East, and their general managers are all based in Shanghai. Even Japanese steamship companies, in addition to their head offices, consider Shanghai a first-class branch office. Ports such as Hong Kong and Dalian are under the jurisdiction of the Shanghai office. Since Japan forcibly occupied the four northeastern provinces of China and established the puppet state of Manchukuo, Japanese goods have been boycotted by China, and the organizational structure of Japanese shipping companies has also changed due to the shifting situation. Shanghai, which the Japanese have regarded as a base for developing shipping for decades, is now being moved to Dalian in one fell swoop, with Shanghai being reduced to a third-class district and undergoing downsizing. The changes in Japanese shipping companies in Shanghai are recorded as follows:

Easy Export of Grains Transferred 172

Of the millions of tons of Northeastern soybeans and other grains shipped annually from Europe and the United States, 60-70% were traditionally transshipped through Shanghai. Even those directly shipped to Dalian for loading only paid customs duties once. Starting from September 25th of last year, the puppet state forcibly seized control of customs duties in the Northeast, resulting in a double tax on soybeans and other grains, which then disappeared from the trade routes to Shanghai. European and American buyers of these grains have had to change their shipping locations, no longer transshipping through Shanghai, and instead loading directly. Competition in the shipping industry has also arisen as a result.

Japanese Merchants Seize Shipping Rights 173

At the beginning of the Japanese occupation of the Northeast, Japanese shipping companies, under the direction of their government, aimed to develop Manchuria and Mongolia and expand exports. They rushed to seize priority in Northeastern shipping. Long-distance transportation was limited to Nippon Yusen, Osaka Shosen, and Mitsui Lines. Short-sea transportation was taken over by Dalian Kisen. Each steamship company competed to build new ships to travel from the Northeast to Europe and the United States, and the first-class branch office in Shanghai was moved to Dalian, while Shanghai was reorganized and reduced to a third-class branch. Nippon Yusen's six express ships were built for this new route. Nippon Yusen, Osaka Shosen, and other companies have added Dalian to their routes to Europe, America, and Australia to transport Northeastern export goods. Several Japanese ships have already cancelled their Shanghai voyages. Originally, Dalian and other locations were under the jurisdiction of the Shanghai branch, but now they are all managed by Dalian.

Shanghai Office Restructures 174

The Japanese steamship branch offices in Shanghai have all been downgraded from first-class to third-class. According to their organizational regulations, the number of personnel used is also being reduced by half. The remaining employees in Shanghai are being transferred to Dalian. All Japanese steamship companies in this port are in the process of complying with these changes. Previously, only those who had served as the head of the Shanghai branch could be promoted to the president of the Japanese head office. Now, it is becoming necessary to have served as the head of the Dalian branch to be promoted to president of the head office, and Shanghai has been downgraded in importance.

Changes in Osaka Shosen Kaisha President 175

The Osaka Shosen Kaisha in this port has received instructions from the head office to reorganize. Watanabe Tokukichi, the president of the Shanghai branch, has been transferred to become the president of the Dalian branch. Inoue Akio, who was in the New York division, has been transferred to become the president of the Shanghai branch. With Shanghai reorganized as a third-class branch, the employees who are to be laid off will be taken by Watanabe to the Dalian branch. Watanabe has already handed over his duties yesterday, and Inoue has taken over. From now on, the management and development objectives of Japanese shipping in China will shift from Shanghai to the Northeast. This is a noteworthy record of the changes in Japanese shipping to China.

Scatter Flowers 179

The lottery will be drawn at 1 PM. The steel lottery machines used for this lottery have been properly dispatched by the British-owned Ruirong Company, totaling three machines, A, B, and C, with machine B being the largest, and machines A and C being equal in size. When the lottery is drawn, in addition to sending letters of invitation to the Shanghai District Court, the First Special District Court, the Second Special District Court, and other government offices, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Bankers' Association, and other official French representatives to supervise, the public will be allowed to enter the venue to observe at will, without selling tickets or imposing any restrictions. As for these 500,000 lottery tickets, if they cannot all be sold, the remaining number will be purchased by the Ministry of Finance. Therefore, these lottery tickets will always be considered sold out.

Explanation of Lottery Drawing 180

The office is currently issuing an explanation of the lottery drawing in Chinese and English, stating that three steel lottery machines will be used. These three machines are all installed on iron bases, with a semi-circular steel frame around the machine, so they can rotate freely. Inside the machine, there are multiple wooden toggles and steel teeth. When the machine rotates, the wooden toggles move the small balls inside the machine, causing them to pass through the copper teeth and be evenly stirred. Each machine has a spring-loaded door at the top and bottom that opens when triggered, releasing the small ball into a glass container. 1. Machine A. Machine A has 667 small balls, one engraved with the character "Deng" (meaning First Prize), two engraved with "Er" (Second Prize), four engraved with "San" (Third Prize), ten engraved with "Si" (Fourth Prize), fifty engraved with "Wu" (Fifth Prize), one hundred engraved with "Liu" (Sixth Prize), and five hundred engraved with "Qi" (Seventh Prize). The number of small balls in machine A matches the number of winning tickets from First Prize to Seventh Prize, totaling 667. 2. Machine B. Machine B has 5,000 small balls, engraved with numbers from 0000 to 4999, representing the first four digits of the winning ticket number, totaling 5,000 numbers. 3. Machine C. Machine C has 100 small balls, engraved with numbers from 00 to 99, representing the last two digits of the winning ticket number, totaling 100 numbers. When the lottery is drawn, in addition to the supervisory committee dispatched by the National Government's Aviation Highway Construction Lottery Committee, representatives from the local court, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and the Bankers' Association will be invited to supervise. The hall will be opened half an hour before the drawing, welcoming people from all walks of life to inspect the machines and small balls. After the inspection is complete, the small balls will be placed in the machines. After the machines have been rotated multiple times to ensure the small balls are stirred evenly, the spring on the door will be released, allowing one small ball to flow out. The numbers drawn from machines B and C will be combined to form the winning ticket number. The number drawn from machine A will be the prize level. The numbers on the small balls drawn from machines B and C will be reported and recorded, and then re-entered into the machines. However, the numbers on the small balls drawn from machine A will not be re-entered, until all 660 small balls in machine A have been drawn, at which point the lottery will be completed. The Eighth Prize and Ninth Prize are those whose last one or two digits are the same as the First Prize number and are not drawn separately. Prizes will be awarded seven days after the drawing (August 7th). As for the lottery drawing method, here is an example: If the number drawn from machine B is 0034, and the number drawn from machine C is 29, and the number drawn from machine A is 3, then lottery ticket number 003429 wins the Third Prize, worth 50,000 yuan.

Second Issue 181

The second issue of the Aviation Highway Construction Lottery has now been printed, and sales will begin simultaneously in all locations on August 1st. The number of provinces selling the lottery will be greater than the first time, but remote areas with poor transportation will still be difficult to sell in.

Flower Gambling Will Harass Landlords 194

The Police in Charge Should Take Responsibility First

Wen Hongen, the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, previously ordered a strict investigation and prosecution of flower gambling, which was rampant in the territory. However, offenders continued to commit offenses and secretly established listening posts and shipping companies to collect gambling money. Director Wen issued a notice stating that anyone found to be operating a flower gambling establishment would have the owner of the house arrested and prosecuted. He then submitted a request to the Municipal Government for approval. It is now heard that the Municipal Government has instructed the director to comply. According to the original order, which is roughly as follows, "Whether the landlord knew that the property was leased for use as a gambling venue and whether the landlord intended to profit from it are both factual and legal issues. The landlord cannot be arrested and prosecuted simply because a flower gambling establishment is discovered. Furthermore, it is customary in Shanghai that most property owners have rental agents to manage everything. If the rental agent has violated the trust of the property owner and leased the property for use as a gambling venue, then the fault lies with the rental agent, and the property owner should not be held responsible. The fault lies with the rental agent. In the future, if the bureau encounters such cases, it should investigate carefully, determine the facts, and dispose of the matter according to law, to avoid harming the innocent." It is heard that Director Wen has instructed his subordinates to comply with the order.

Prohibiting Foreigners from Filming Movies 196

Must Comply with Our Country's Film Regulations

The Film Censorship Committee, in view of the endless instances of foreign merchants venturing deeply into our country's interior to privately film movies, a matter concerning international propaganda and national honor, and of no small consequence, has specially drafted regulations for foreigners filming movies in China. These regulations have been submitted to the Ministry of Interior for review and approval, with instructions for strict enforcement by all police agencies across the country. It is understood that the Municipal Government has received the internal request and has instructed the Municipal Public Security Bureau to comply. The regulations are as follows: (Article 1) All foreigners filming movies within the Republic of China must comply with these regulations. (Article 2) Foreigners filming movies in China must possess a passport for travel in the interior issued by the Chinese government. (Article 3) Foreigners filming movies in China must present their passport for travel in the interior and obtain a permit from the local police agency, requesting that personnel be assigned for supervision. (Article 4) After issuing a permit and assigning personnel to supervise the filming, the police agency shall fill out a form prepared by the Film Censorship Committee and submit it to the Film Censorship Committee for record. (Article 5) Foreigners filming movies in China shall avoid the following circumstances in their material: (1) Events that damage the dignity of the Chinese nation, (2) Performances that violate the Three Principles of the People, (3) Customs that are not in line with the good morals of this country, (4) Events that contain superstition or the bizarre. (Article 6) After a film is produced, it must be submitted to the Film Censorship Committee for inspection and approval before it can be exported. (Article 7) These regulations shall take effect from the date of approval by the Executive Yuan.

French Concession Police Issue Orders to Strictly Arrest the Morphine King 197

The morphine king, Zhang Zhongguo (formerly mistakenly reported as Zhong Han), a native of Ningbo, and his brother Zhang Zhonghai, initially opened the Zhongxing Inn next to the Catholic Church at the west end of Laobeimen on Min'guo Road in the French Concession. They accumulated capital by dealing in opium and, in four or five years, amassed assets of hundreds of thousands, becoming extremely wealthy. Their morphine manufacturing facilities were previously located in the International Settlement and in the countryside west of Shanghai. Due to their secrecy, they were never discovered by officials, allowing them to operate freely and profit. Recently, due to strict crackdowns in both the Chinese and International settlements, they could no longer operate there. They initially intended to shut down and cease operations to avoid scrutiny, but because they still had unfinished raw materials worth approximately thirty to forty thousand gold coins, the Zhangs thought the sum was too large to abandon. Therefore, on the first of this month, they moved from the International Settlement to No. 5, Xia Linli, Zhengjia Muqiao Street in the French Concession, planning to sell off the remaining inventory before closing down. They utilized the rooftop platform of the three-story building, constructing four small wooden rooms to house the machinery and motors for manufacturing. To avoid attracting attention, workers used thick hemp ropes to ascend and descend. All incoming and outgoing goods and accounts were managed by Zhongguo's daughter, A'cui, who supervised the work day and night, rushing to finish within a month before moving on to other ventures. Unexpectedly, on the seventh of this month, Chief Inspector Jin Jiulin of the French Concession's Special Bureau and Detective Wang Zhihao discovered their operation and raided the premises at 10 PM. The Zhang brothers were out and had not returned, but they captured eight workers: Yu Jinfu, Zhou Xuewen, Ye Ronggen, Fei Xianggen, Wang A'er, Wu Mingsheng (real name Yu Mingchun), Jiang A'si, and Chen Li'shi. They seized motors, machinery, twenty-two "chi" of finished morphine, and four lead buckets of unfinished raw materials. The items were sent to the Second Special Court for prosecution. After a trial presided over by Judge Wang Gangxu, the verdict is scheduled to be announced today. Previous reports have briefly covered these events. It is now understood that the "king" brothers and their daughter escaped the dragnet and remain at large. In order to eradicate drugs and eliminate evil, the police authorities have instructed all detectives to investigate within the concession for any secretly established facilities of this kind and immediately arrest and bring them to justice. Simultaneously, an arrest warrant has been issued, ordering all detectives to closely investigate and apprehend the escaped morphine king, the Zhang brothers, their daughter, and bring them to justice for interrogation.

War Zone Bonds to be Issued Next Month 198

Procedures Already Prepared

According to the Central News Agency, the central government decided to allocate five million yuan for the relief of the North China war zone. Of this amount, one million yuan was allocated as cash and remitted. The remaining four million yuan will be used by the Ministry of Finance to issue relief bonds for the North China war zone, secured by the Changlu salt tax. This has been reported in the newspapers. According to sources in the local banking community, the procedures for issuing these bonds have been completed, and they will be issued next month. Rumors that the issuance will be delayed until Minister Song returns to the country are inaccurate, as the need for relief funds is urgent. The issuance location has been decided as the banking community of Peiping and Tianjin. Reports that they will be issued in Shanghai are also untrue.

After the resignation of Mr. Chen Zhongsheng, Director of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Fisheries Administration, the ministry has appointed Yuan Lianghua to take over. It is reported that Mr. Yuan has decided to proceed to take charge on August 1st.

Robbery on Route D'Eliseé 200

The Yichengxin rice store, located at 432, the intersection of Route D'Eliseé and Miaohou Road, in Zhabei, and owned by He Bingshan from Pinghu, was suddenly visited by six robbers at 3:30 AM yesterday. One stood guard outside the door, while the other five broke into the store, brandished pistols, and monitored everyone inside, preventing them from moving or making noise. The robbers then looted as they pleased, taking cash, clothing, and jewelry, totaling over one hundred yuan. After obtaining the loot, they fled. When the robbers were committing the robbery, the store owner resisted slightly and was struck several times on the head by the robber with the gun handle, causing head injuries and bleeding. After the incident, he reported to the Third Precinct of the Fifth District, requesting an investigation. The injured person went to the hospital for treatment.

Robbery on Route Sicawei - One Thief Apprehended on the Spot 201

The Tongyihe tobacco and paper shop, located at 245 Route Sicawei in the French Concession, and owned by Sun Shifu from Shaoxing, was suddenly visited by four robbers at 8 AM the day before yesterday. Three were wearing short blue cloth jackets, and one was wearing a white Indian silk long gown. They were armed with pistols and forbade anyone from making noise. Three robbers stood guard outside the door, while one robber inside grabbed thirty yuan in silver dollars and ninety cents in small silver coins from the drawer of the accounts table and fled. The apprentice chased after them, shouting for help. The robbers fired three shots in resistance, but fortunately, no one was injured. Chief Detective Lu Zhulin and Deputy Detective Zhang Daorong of the French Concession Police and patrol officers arrived on the scene after hearing the alert. They chased the robbers to the vicinity of Xinxinli near Dapu Bridge, where they apprehended one of the robbers, Huang A'xiang (30 years old). The other robbers escaped without a trace. Huang was taken to the police station and yesterday was escorted to the First Criminal Division of the Second Special Court. The police lawyer, Gu Shouxi, stated the facts of the case, briefly saying that the police had not yet completed the investigation and the accomplices had not been apprehended, requesting a postponement of the interrogation. Huang A'xiang confessed to going to commit the crime with the three escaped robbers, including Hu A'xiang, and did not deny it. After verification of the confession by Judge Xiong Hui, the trial was postponed to August 1st, and he was remanded in custody.

Regulations for Foreign Merchants Renting Chinese Ships 202

Draft

The Shanghai Navigation Bureau believes that foreign merchants renting Chinese ships do not register, operate inland, and arbitrarily lower prices, which is detrimental to our shipping industry. In order to limit this, the Bureau has requested the Ministry of Communications to issue an order stipulating that foreign merchants renting Chinese ships must apply to the competent navigation authority for registration and must follow the procedures for foreign ships applying for inland port licenses before they can operate in inland ports. It is understood that the Ministry of Communications has approved this and has ordered the Bureau to draft regulations for foreign merchants renting Chinese ships and submit them to the Ministry for review and decision. The Bureau has begun drafting the regulations. It is also reported that the Ministry of Communications, for ease of enforcement, will prepare a license for foreign merchants renting Chinese ships. All foreign merchants renting Chinese ships operating in inland ports must apply for a license for use; those without a license will not be allowed to clear customs.

Two People Die by Suicide 203

Ren Laosan, a 38-year-old man from Suzhou, lived at No. 7, Guixiang Lane, Dagu Road, Xiaoximen, Nanshi. Yesterday at around 10 AM, he was driven to despair by prolonged unemployment and economic hardship, leading him to swallow raw opium in an attempt to take his own life. His family discovered him and rushed him to Renji Hospital for treatment, but due to an overdose, treatment was ineffective, and he died at around 6 PM. He was transferred to the coroner's office for autopsy.

Wen Genbao, a 23-year-old woman from Suzhou, lived at No. 9, Zengyong Lane, Glock Road, in the French Concession. Yesterday at 9 AM, she had an argument with her husband over a trivial matter. Unable to vent her anger, she became despondent and swallowed opium in secret. Her family found Wen looking lifeless and moaning on the bed, knowing she must have taken poison. They quickly hired a vehicle to take her to Renji Hospital, but due to severe poisoning, treatment was ineffective, and she died at around 10 AM. She was transferred to the coroner's office for autopsy.

Sincerely, Preparatory Committee of the Chinese Seamen's Union, July 28.

Students Failing One Non-Core Subject in Joint Entrance Exams Allowed Flexible Admission 210

The Ministry of Education previously received a request from the Jiangsu Education Department. The Ministry has now instructed the Department that high school graduates taking the joint entrance exam who fail one subject other than Chinese, English, Mathematics, Physics, or Chemistry may be issued a certificate by the Department to apply for specialized schools or higher institutions as probationary students. Those failing the junior high school joint entrance exam may apply as students with equivalent qualifications.

Jiangsu Province Establishes Elementary Education Supervisors in Teacher Training Districts 213

An instruction from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education states: It has been decided that in order to actively guide local elementary schools to improve, the department previously stipulated that local education supervisors be established within the provincial middle schools' experimental elementary schools to guide improvement by district. Methods were established and promulgated. Last year, teacher training districts were established, and in accordance with Article 7 of the Outline of the Jiangsu Provincial Teacher Training Education Improvement Plan, each teacher training district should establish two to three local education supervisors. Although their specific duties are not explicitly defined, their goal is to guide local education. Now, some middle school experimental elementary schools have been converted into affiliated elementary schools following the teacher training schools, and the previously promulgated methods for guiding local education are no longer applicable. Based on the Outline of the Jiangsu Provincial Teacher Training Education Improvement Plan, eight articles of the Provisional Measures for the Establishment of Elementary Education Supervisors in Jiangsu Province Teacher Training Districts have been drafted and passed by the 587th meeting of the Jiangsu Provincial Government Committee. In addition to separate orders, the measures are issued herewith. The principals of the schools are instructed to comply and promptly distribute the measures to the principals of the affiliated schools to select two qualified and capable personnel and submit their names for review and appointment to begin work. The original local education supervisors in the affiliated elementary schools will be abolished. This order must be obeyed.

Provisional Measures for the Establishment of Elementary Education Supervisors in Jiangsu Province Teacher Training Districts

Article 1: In order to actively improve elementary education in various counties, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, in accordance with Article 7 of the Outline of the Jiangsu Provincial Teacher Training Education Improvement Plan, establishes two or three elementary education supervisors within the affiliated elementary schools of each teacher training school to guide elementary education in each teacher training district.

Article 2: Elementary education supervisors should, under the direction of the principal of the teacher training school in each teacher training district and in consultation with the principal of the affiliated elementary school, participate in elementary education research work at the school and conduct circuit inspections of elementary education within each teacher training district. Their research and inspection tasks are listed as follows:

A. Regarding research:

(1) Assist in the experimental research of the duty plan of the research department of the affiliated elementary school of each teacher training school.

(2) Handle research matters designated by the principal of each teacher training school and the principal of the affiliated elementary school, and prepare reports at any time.

(3) Compile statistics on elementary education surveys within each teacher training district.

(4) Edit guidance publications based on the actual needs of each teacher training district.

(5) Participate in in-service training for guidance teachers within each teacher training district.

(6) Attend important meetings of each teacher training school and affiliated elementary school.

(7) Participate in elementary education research in each county within each teacher training district.

(8) Attend the Elementary Education Improvement Research Conference in each teacher training district.

B. Regarding inspection:

(1) Each person must inspect elementary education in each county within each teacher training district for one week each academic year, and inspect at least 150 elementary schools each semester. However, the schools inspected must be as comprehensive as possible, avoiding duplication. The distribution of regions will be designated by the principals of the affiliated elementary schools of each teacher training school.

(2) When inspecting each school, detailed guidance should be given on points that need improvement in administrative organization, environmental arrangement, grade composition, curriculum arrangement, and teaching methods.

(3) After completing the inspection of each school, in addition to convening talks with the principal and teachers, the main points of guidance must be extracted, and the principal of the school must improve according to the guidance.

(4) After completing the inspection of each school district, a guidance meeting should be held with the principals and teachers in the district to discuss or answer practical problems in administration and teaching. Demonstration teaching may be held when necessary.

(5) After completing the inspection of each county, opinions on elementary education improvement should be submitted to the director of the county education bureau or the county head and the Elementary Education Improvement Research Conference of the teacher training district.

(6) Before the end of each semester, in consultation with the principal of the affiliated elementary school, a work log for this semester, inspection reports, records of guidance meetings, and opinions on elementary education improvement in each county in the teacher training district should be prepared, together with a work plan for the next semester, and submitted to the principal of the teacher training school for submission to the Department of Education for verification and processing. Special circumstances may be reported at any time for submission to the Department of Education for verification and processing.

(7) Other matters.

Article 3: Elementary education supervisors will be selected by the principal of the teacher training school in each teacher training district in conjunction with the principal of the affiliated elementary school, and those who meet one of the following qualifications will be submitted to the Department of Education for approval and appointment. When submitting a recommendation, a resume, supporting documents, a plan, and works must be submitted. When necessary, the Department of Education may directly appoint them.

A. Graduates of education departments, teacher training universities, or higher normal schools at home and abroad who have conducted research on elementary education.

B. Graduates of senior high school teacher training programs or teacher training undergraduate programs who have served in experimental elementary schools or affiliated elementary schools for more than three years and have achieved results in research and experimentation.

Article 4: The salary of elementary education supervisors is 60 to 80 yuan per month per person, depending on the knowledge and experience of each person. Travel expenses will be reimbursed based on actual expenses, and shall not exceed 300 yuan for the whole year, except in special circumstances and with approved submission.

Article 5: Elementary education supervisors should be employed for a long term in principle. If they are found to be ineffective or give inadequate guidance, the Department of Education, after investigation, or the principal of the teacher training school, after submitting a factual report, should dismiss them.

Article 6: When provincial supervisors inspect elementary education in the teacher training district, elementary education supervisors should explain the general situation of elementary education in each county in the district and provide opinions on improvement. Provincial supervisors should separately assess the work performance of the supervisor.

Article 7: When elementary education supervisors go to various counties for inspection, county supervisors and education committee members should assist at any time and attend the convened guidance meetings. They must also supervise the schools to implement the proposed improvement opinions at any time.

Article 8: These measures will be implemented upon the decision of the Jiangsu Provincial Government Committee and will be filed with the Ministry of Education for record.

Local News

Private Secondary Schools to Stop Enrolling Normal School Students Starting in the 22nd Academic Year 219

Existing Students Will Continue Until Graduation

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued an instruction to the city's private secondary schools yesterday, stating that starting from the 22nd year of the Republic of China (i.e., starting from the autumn of 1933), all private secondary schools in the city that also run normal school departments must not enroll new freshmen or transfer students. Existing students will continue until graduation. This bureau has already ordered compliance with this rule. It has been found that some school enrollment advertisements still advertise for new freshmen and transfer students for the normal school departments, which is very inappropriate. To avoid long-term negligence, this bureau reiterates the previous order. In the future, if there are any violations of the law, this bureau will definitely ban it. This order must be obeyed.

Universal Student Association and Others Actively Preparing to Welcome Overseas Students 220

The Venue for the Farewell Party Will Be Changed to a More Suitable Location

Plans to Hold a Forum for Overseas Students and Publish a Special Edition

Dongwu Alumni Association Hoster a Farewell Banquet for Students Going Abroad Yesterday

The annual farewell party for students going abroad is being jointly organized this year by the Universal Chinese Student Association, the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education, and local cultural organizations. It is scheduled to be held at 4:00 PM on August 13th. The venue was originally scheduled to be Mayor Wu's Garden on Haig Road, but it is heard that the renovation has not been completed, and a more suitable location may be changed. It will be announced again at that time. Here is a summary of the latest preparations:

To Hold a Forum for Overseas Students. In order to help overseas students understand the situation abroad, the association has decided to hold a forum for overseas students before the welcome party to guide all matters related to going abroad and introduce customs, schools' latest conditions, and all the procedures required for admission in various countries. All students going abroad this year are welcome to attend. The date of the forum has not yet been determined, but it will be held around August 10th. Also, the invitations to the farewell party will still be distributed by the association. Students residing in this city who are preparing to go abroad are requested to send their mailing addresses to the association so that the invitations can be distributed to avoid omissions.

Publish a Special Edition for Overseas Students. To facilitate overseas students' reading, the association has started editing a special edition for overseas students. The content is divided into three columns: (1) Writings of predecessors in the overseas student community; (2) Overseas study guidance, from applying for a passport to boarding a ship and going abroad until enrolling in school. All procedures and necessary procedures are recorded in detail; (3) Overseas student survey. There is a precise survey and statistics of official and private-funded overseas students from all schools across the country in the year from July last year to June this year. It is scheduled to be published before August 10th for distribution at the conference.

Overseas Student Statistics. The Universal Student Association published the following simple statistics for overseas students in the 21st year: 230 students studying in Japan, 103 students studying in France, 80 students studying in the United States, 68 students studying in Germany, 50 students studying in the United Kingdom, 12 students studying in Belgium, 2 students studying in Austria, 1 student studying in Canada, 1 student studying in Poland, and 1 student studying in India, for a total of 548 students.

Dongwu hosted a farewell banquet yesterday. The graduating class of the Law School of Dongwu University on Kunshan Road in this city hosted a farewell banquet for students going abroad at the Zhongshe on Weihaiwei Road yesterday. More than 200 guests attended. Huang Zhaohong, Wang Qipei, Zhang Yifan, Qi Zhanfan, Xue Guangqian, and Yin Qinqin of the alumni association provided warm hospitality. During the banquet, Dr. Liang Yunli, a graduate of the college, a specialist member of the Chinese delegation to the Geneva Convention, and the newly appointed Counselor of the Executive Yuan, gave a speech on "Research on International Doctrines," which was concise and profound, and moved the audience. He especially encouraged the students going abroad this time. After the speech, Feng Xigeng was elected by the students going abroad to give a thank you speech, and the meeting did not disperse until after 9:00. The students going abroad this time include Feng Xigeng, Ying Wangyong, Wang Jieyuan, Huang Zhensheng, Zeng Menghiong, Zheng Guonan, and more than a dozen others. Most of them will enter universities in the UK, the United States, and France to study law. The admission procedures have been completed. The departure date is around the beginning of September.

The Disaster Relief Association for Secondary Schools in This City Subsidizes Daogang and Anhui Schools with Relief Funds 223

The Disaster Relief Association for Secondary Schools in the Shanghai "January 28th" War Zone consists of 13 schools, including Aiguo Girls' High School, Jianguo Middle School, Fudan Experimental Middle School, Lida Academy, Nanyang Commercial High School, Guangdong Middle School, Shanghai North Middle School, Minsheng Middle School, Xinmin Middle School, Chizhi Affiliated Middle School, China Women's Physical Education Normal School, Daogang Girls' Middle School, and Anhui Middle School. All of them suffered heavy disasters, and have repeatedly applied to the Municipal Bureau of Education and the War Zone Relief Committee for remedies, and have received several batches of relief funds. However, only Daogang and Anhui schools have not received this relief fund because they have not been registered. Although the association has repeatedly requested the authorities, it has not been approved. The association believes that since the two schools are both members of the association and have suffered roughly the same disasters, how can they be left out? Therefore, there is a resolution to subsidize them. It is heard that the method is to take the school with the lowest amount of relief funds as the standard, and then distribute it equally according to the amount received by each school to subsidize them. The two schools can each receive 360 yuan. In addition, because the amount received by the school that has already received it cannot be less than the amount received by the school that is subsidized, the school with the least amount received will no longer be required to contribute funds for subsidies to show fairness. It is also heard that the method has been properly allocated by the association's standing committee, and fees will be collected from each school that should contribute. Once the fees are collected, they will be handed over to Daogang and Anhui schools to clear the procedures and end the matter.

Liu Xuesong Advocates That Tsinghua Should Send Students to the US to Study Physical Education 250

Liu Xuesong expressed his thoughts on Tsinghua's recent recruitment of students for studying in the US. He said that he read in the newspaper that Tsinghua's regulations for recruiting students to study in the US are limited to literature, science, engineering, and agriculture, and there is no special quota for physical education. Xuesong, having just returned from the US, deeply feels that the reason why people in that country are energetic and diligent in their work is largely due to their strong physical constitution. To achieve a strong physical constitution, one cannot succeed without physical education. Last year, the National Sports Conference was held in Beijing, and the petition to the Ministry of Education to send students to study physical education in the US was approved. Now that Tsinghua is recruiting students, it is a good opportunity to seek advanced studies for domestic physical education talents, but the Ministry of Education has not paid attention to this, which is a pity. When I was studying at Springfield, the Japanese government sent a government-funded student, but in our country, there was no such thing. After returning to China, Springfield University specially set up a free scholarship for our country, with an honorary award, and has contacted me to introduce students. Other countries' schools are even more encouraging to us, but the domestic authorities turn a blind eye, which is puzzling. The strength of an individual's physique and the rise and fall of a nation are all dependent on the prosperity of physical education. The weakness of the Chinese people's physique and the decline of the nation are already so obvious. If we still do not emphasize physical education, I fear that in a few decades, there will be no place for us in the international community. I believe that the sports community should strive for this based on reason to promote the authorities' advocacy.

Athletic Achievements of Zhijiang College of Arts and Sciences 251

Since the resumption of Zhijiang College of Arts and Sciences four years ago, there have been many noteworthy developments in physical education. Here is a summary of the main points. In the autumn of 1929, when the school resumed, there were more than 300 students in four grades in the high school and college departments. The funding for physical education was sufficient to maintain operations. In the winter of that year, the school joined the Hangzhou A-League football competition and won the championship. The following spring, the school held its first all-school sports meet, with excellent results and high spirits. The school won the overall championship in the first Zhejiang Provincial Games and track and field events, which was quite a sensation at the time. In the same year, when the province selected representatives for the National Games, the players of various sports teams were mainly from our school, which quickly gained a reputation and spread to Beijing and Shanghai. In the autumn of 1930, in the four-university volleyball competition, the school defeated the powerful Shanghai University team in Suzhou. In the winter of the same year, the school won two Hangzhou football championships and was runner-up in the four-university football competition. In the spring of 1931, the four-university basketball competition was held at our school, with the school, Shanghai University, and Jinling University sharing the championship, forming a three-way balance. In the autumn, our province held the second Zhejiang Provincial Games, and our school won the championship again. There were many talented people, which was a great success at the time. In the winter of the same year, the Northeast Incident occurred, and students engaged in military training, so they did not have time to focus on sports activities. At the same time, the focus of physical education gradually shifted from athlete training to general physical education, in order to seek balanced development. This year, the equipment was greatly expanded, with the addition of clubs, dumbbells, pommel horses, parallel bars, and training for freehand exercises, apparatus exercises, and swimming exercises during classes, so that all students could get proper physical training. It should be known that the progress of a school's physical education is not only measured by a few athletes, but by the healthy physique of all students. Therefore, the purpose of physical education training is not only to train athletes to win championships, but to enable everyone to have a strong physique and a healthy body and mind, in order to promote the true spirit of physical education. Looking back on the past four years, the physical education work of our college has made great progress, and its reputation has spread far and wide. The facilities have also been gradually enriched, including more than a dozen football fields, track and field fields, basketball, tennis, and volleyball courts, as well as a gymnasium and a swimming pool. The sports equipment has also been increased and enriched. Liu Xuesong is currently in charge of physical education, and in the future, he will focus on developing universal physical education, cultivating the healthy physique of young people, and promoting the strength of the nation.

Simple Method for Calculating Wire 254

—Yi Zhi

Before winding coils or making cages, the first step is to determine which gauge wire to use, the number of turns per hour, the length per pound, and the safe current load. If you have a wire table on hand, you can find the information immediately. However, if you do not have a wire table on hand, finding a wire table or asking someone is troublesome. Now, there is a simple method for calculating wire that is easy to understand and easy to remember. By following this method, the calculated results will be only slightly different from the values in the wire table. I will now describe this method in detail below.

The wire gauges used in the world are all based on the American Standard Wire Gauge (AWG) table, with the English abbreviation B&S. The table lists the wire gauge, diameter, cross-sectional area, number of turns per hour, length per pound, and safe current load for checking and application. Now, by using this simple calculation method, you can calculate all the items listed on the table. I will explain them separately below.

(1) Finding the Wire Gauge

The wire gauge table has numbers from 1 to 45. Above number 1, there are also number 4, with distinctions made by using one zero, two zeros, etc. In this wire gauge table, the cross-sectional area of each wire gauge has a constant incremental number. For every three gauge numbers larger, the cross-sectional area increases by two times. For every three gauge numbers smaller, the cross-sectional area decreases by half. For every ten gauge numbers larger, the cross-sectional area increases by ten times. For every ten gauge numbers smaller, the cross-sectional area decreases by one-tenth. For example, the cross-sectional area of a 20-gauge wire in the table is 1022 circular mils (Circular Mils; one mil equals one-thousandth of an inch). Therefore, the cross-sectional area of a 17-gauge wire is 1022 x 2 = 2044 circular mils, and the cross-sectional area of a 23-gauge wire is 1022 x 0.5 = 511 circular mils. Therefore, knowing the cross-sectional area allows you to know the gauge number. Example: A wire has a cross-sectional area of 50 circular mils. What is the gauge number of this wire?

Solution: Since we know that the cross-sectional area of a 30-gauge wire is 100 circular mils, 50 ÷ 100 = 0.5 determines that it is a 33-gauge wire.

(2) Finding the Diameter

Take the square root of the cross-sectional area. The square root is the value of the diameter because the cross-sectional area is the product of the diameter multiplied by itself.

Example: A certain gauge wire has a cross-sectional area of 1022 circular mils. What is the diameter of this wire?

Solution: √1022 = 32 mils (to be continued)

Design of Coil Isolation Shield 255

—Shi Qiwei

In radio receivers, coils and capacitors are densely distributed and interconnected. It is difficult to avoid mutual magnetic and electrical inductance, which reduces the efficiency of each circuit and can even cause them to malfunction. Therefore, radio designers and manufacturers strive to avoid this magnetic inductance. The most effective way to do this is to use an isolation shield. Without discussing other parts, I will only study the isolation shield used for the coil. The shield must be made of a good conductive sheet, preferably aluminum or copper. The form, distance, and dimensions of the shield and the coil should be as follows: A is the shield, E is the metal base plate, D is the L-shaped metal, and C is the coil and shield.

The distance between

the coil and shield

should be more than

one inch.

The distance between B should be more than one-half of the diameter of the coil.

Measuring Resistance 256

—Qi

Most readers probably remember the article "Homemade High Resistance" in this publication. However, to determine its resistance accurately, you must use an instrument. If the resistance is very high, the current passing through it will also be very small. Using the ordinary method (as shown in the first diagram) will not be accurate, and the resistance that you want to measure will be limited. Exceeding the range will prevent you from measuring the accurate resistance.

However, by following the method described below, you can measure resistances from as small as a few ohms to as large as hundreds of thousands of ohms. The first diagram shows the ordinary method. AB are the connecting terminals, E is the battery, and the voltage does not have to be 1.5 volts; it can be higher. There is also a 0.1MA ammeter or a 0.10MA ammeter, but the former is more accurate. R is the resistance to be measured. According to Ohm's Law, R = E/I, so R must be at least Rx = 1.5/0.001 = or higher; otherwise, the current passing through it will exceed the range of the ammeter, and therefore you will not be able to determine its resistance. If you add a variable resistor to the above circuit (second diagram), short-circuit the AB terminals, and adjust the variable resistor R until the meter shows the maximum current, then separate the AB terminals. In this way, you can measure resistances of 100 ohms or higher. That is, R× = E/I - R. If the resistance to be measured is extremely high, you can increase the voltage of the battery E, but the resistance of R must also be changed. For example, if E is 1.5 volts, then R must be approximately R = E/.001-1.5

00.

The third diagram is for measuring resistances below 100 ohms. The function of R is the same as above, but this time, the AB terminals are not short-circuited, and the meter is made to show the maximum current. At this time, connect R, and you can use the following formula to calculate its resistance.

Rx = R/m - n - i

Rm is the resistance of the meter. For example, the meter mentioned above is approximately 30 ohms.

n is the ratio of the maximum current on the meter to the current indicated on the meter.

For example:

Rm = 30

Current indicated on the meter = 0.75MA

Then R × = (approximately)

Small Experience

Power Plug 257

—Zhenzhi

In AC radios, sometimes reversing the power plug can improve the reception, which is very strange. Although the positive and negative ends of the AC circuit alternate in time, the plug has a fixed way to insert it. Often, inserting it this way is correct, and inserting it that way is incorrect. Current flowing into your radio from one direction may perform better than current flowing in from the other direction. By repeatedly reversing the plug, you can test for a better current direction.

Try plugging your power plug in and out several times; you will be able to find a better way to insert it. Once you have found it, make corresponding marks on the plug and the socket, such as a small groove. Then, apply some white powder to the groove so that it is easy to identify when changing the position of the plug.

Substitute for Winding Machine 丨Grinding Wheel Frame丨Jin Yunchiao 258

When making transformers, a winding machine is indispensable. It is not only faster than winding by hand but also more even. However, it seems too uneconomical to spend money to buy a winding machine just to wind one or two coils. A grinding wheel frame is an excellent substitute for a winding machine. You can borrow one from a metalworker, loosen the cap nut, remove the grinding wheel, and then install a wooden shaft made of a suitable iron core. Tighten the cap nut, and you can apply it. (Note: The handle of the grinding wheel frame and the rotation direction of the grinding wheel are often opposite; therefore, you must crank it in reverse to wind the coil. The iron sheet next to the grinding wheel should also be removed to avoid scratching the enameled wire.)

Method for Identifying Fixed Resistors 259

—Chen Qibei

Recently, the resistance of various fixed resistors produced by electrical component factories is not indicated by numbers but is distinguished by colors. I will now list the color counting table published in the United States for purchasers to identify.

The color painted on the entire body is the first number.

One Two Three Four Five Six Seven Eight Nine Zero

The color on the tail end is the second number.

Brown Red Orange Yellow Green Blue Violet Gray White Black

One Two Three Four Five Six Seven Eight Nine Zero

The color in the middle waist is the third number.

Black Brown Red Orange Yellow Green Blue

For example, if the color of the body is brown, the color of the tail is green, and the color of the waist is red, then the resistance is 1,500 ohms. The rest can be found in the same way.

Precautions for Using and Charging Storage Batteries 260

—Zhong Shixing

Storage batteries can be divided into lead-acid batteries and nickel-iron batteries. Lead-acid batteries have a higher voltage than nickel-iron batteries, so the use of copper storage batteries is more common. Both are very expensive, and if we protect and use them properly, they can last for many years without breaking.

Storage batteries have a higher voltage when the current is sufficient. After using them for some time, the voltage gradually drops. When the current in a new copper storage battery is sufficient, the voltage is approximately two volts. After using it for some time, it is best not to use it again when the voltage drops to 1.8 volts. When a nickel-iron battery is fully charged, it is 1.4 volts. When it reaches 1 volt, it should no longer be used and must be recharged.

The voltage used in our radios is high, so multiple batteries are connected in series. On storage batteries, the red or ㈩ experience is the mark of the anode, and the black or ㈠ is the mark of the cathode. If we want a higher voltage, we will connect each anode individually. The height of the voltage is proportional to the amount of storage batteries.

The unit of storage battery capacity is called ampere-hours, which is the product of amperes and time. Most of the ones used in radios are 60 ampere-hours.

When we use it to the voltage specified above, we must recharge it. However, regardless of whether you use it or not, it is best to charge it once within a certain period. If it is not used for more than five or six months, you should pour out the liquid inside, wash it very clean with clean water, store the liquid, and put it back in when you need to use it. This way, it can be permanently preserved without breaking.

Charging a new storage battery for the first time is very troublesome, and it takes a relatively long time. It is best to reverse the positive and negative poles. After charging it a few times, you must fix it and not change it again. If we entrust a professional charger to recharge it a few times, it will be easier for us to do it ourselves later.

When charging, if the electrolyte is found to have white boiling foam, it means that it will reach a sufficient state. If the temperature is above 100 degrees Fahrenheit, it is not advisable to charge it again. Wait until it cools down before charging again. Use a liquid specific gravity meter or a voltmeter to measure. The charging voltage for a copper storage battery should be stopped at 1.300, and the voltage should be stopped at 2.6 volts to 2.8 volts. The charging voltage for a nickel-iron battery should be stopped at 1.200, and the voltage should be stopped at 1.5 volts.

At ordinary times, the surface of the storage battery should be wiped clean, and it should not be placed in a damp place. It is best to apply some Vaseline on the lid and put it in another box so that dirt will not accumulate, moisture will not penetrate, and the current will not disappear, and the medicine liquid will not evaporate and stain clothes, etc. The liquid medicine in the storage battery should be immersed on top of the copper plate. If it is dry, you can add distilled water. Do not arbitrarily add liquid medicine or unclean water. If you can use it according to the method, you will definitely be able to receive good results.

Common Knowledge 261

— Huang Jiancun

(11) General Structure of Radios

In recent years, due to the development of broadcast radio, the types of radios are too numerous to count. However, observing their general structure, they are nothing more than the following types:

(1) Antenna Circuit: The radio waves emitted by broadcast radio stations travel in all directions at a speed of approximately 300,000 kilometers per second. At this speed, they can circle the entire Earth more than seven and a half times. If a receiving antenna is installed in the path of the radio waves, the radio waves will be absorbed by the antenna and converted into an oscillating current with a frequency of more than 1.5 million cycles per second, flowing back and forth between the sky and the ground circuit. This type of current has an extremely high frequency and is commonly referred to as high-frequency current or radio-frequency current.

(2) Tuning Circuit: The tuning circuit is the gateway of the radio, consisting of a self-inductance coil and a capacitor. By changing the self-inductance in the coil and the capacitance of the capacitor, the natural frequency of the circuit is increased or decreased to match the radio-frequency symbol frequency that is to be received from the outside. In other words, the tuning circuit is used to select external radio waves. The quality of its manufacturing is sufficient to affect the selectivity and sensitivity of the radio.

(3) Radio-Frequency Amplification Circuit: The radio waves emitted by broadcast radio stations are often too weak due to distance or other reasons, and cannot be used without amplification. The radio-frequency amplification circuit is located between the tuning circuit and the detection circuit and is used to amplify the radio-frequency current.

(4) Detection Circuit: The detection circuit has a detector that acts as a rectifier, converting the radio-frequency current into an audio-frequency current with a lower frequency.

(5) Audio-Frequency Amplification Circuit: This circuit is located after the detection circuit and is used to amplify the audio-frequency current. (6) Output Circuit: In the output circuit, the audio-frequency current is converted into sound, and sound amplifiers and output coupling devices all belong to this circuit.

(7) Power Supply Circuit: The power supply circuit provides power to the radio. For DC radios, the required power source is dry batteries or storage batteries. For AC radios, the power source is the AC power from the lighting wires.

Correction: In the last line of the previous issue's "Common Knowledge," there were "four small squares in the map," which were not printed clearly. A special correction is provided below: "The symbol for grounding is 丨 or 丨, and the symbol for a ground grid is 丨 or 丨."

The Frozen Songhua River 266

— Miaoshen

When the scorching sun is high in the sky and sweat is pouring down like rain, let me talk about the frozen Songhua River, which may be like a cup of ice cream for the readers?

A few years ago, I was in Harbin, next to the Songhua River. At that time, although Harbin belonged to outside the customs, it still flew the Chinese flag. Now, times have changed, and it has become a foreign land. Things are really different now.

The climate in Harbin is very cold. Around the Mid-Autumn Festival, people are about to wear leather clothes. Harbin's water and land transportation is a very large trading port in the three northeastern provinces. When the Songhua River freezes in the cold weather, although ships cannot pass, many ice carts are added to the solid ice. These carts, also known as large carts in the north, can carry more than a thousand catties and are pulled by one or two horses. The carts travel on the ice. Because the ice is slippery, the speed is faster than on land. These carts often travel upstream from Harbin or are pulled from other places, and can travel one or two hundred miles a day. Because of the severe cold on the river, the drivers wear extremely thick old sheepskin coats, leather hats, and leather gloves. The fur of these leather hats and leather gloves is very long and looks quite rough, but it is very warm. There is also a kind of "ice raft" on the ice for people to sit on, also called a "lever." This thing is very simple in construction, with a board placed on two knife-like pieces of iron. The friction between the iron pieces and the ice is very small. People sit on the board, and one person uses a bamboo pole to touch the ice under the crotch. The "ice raft" then moves forward like a flying arrow. However, because the movement is too fast, it is difficult to control, so dangerous things often happen.

After the south bank freezes, there are naturally several air holes in the ice. These air holes are for the fish at the bottom of the ice to breathe. This also shows the intention of God in creating things. Fishermen take advantage of this and put their nets in the holes to fish. Big fish and small fish all come together, which is more labor-saving than when the river is not frozen. This is also something that people generally do not expect.

The ice on the river is several feet thick, and the back of the ice is full of sharp icicles. If someone accidentally falls into the air hole, there is no hope of survival. Therefore, walking on the ice, the air holes are more terrifying than traps. The ice is slippery and difficult to walk on, and being near the air holes is indeed very dangerous.

Water 267

— Xu Xiaoting

All things expand when heated and contract when cooled. China's land, because there are too many friends who are only enthusiastic for five minutes, drink Dutch water and ice without restraint. Throughout this summer, they pour it into their stomachs all day long, cooling their blood! They only care about the shrinking of the land.

Because women are made of water, there are indeed too many fashionable women in the big cities of China. The water content is increasing year by year, becoming more widespread, creating a new record unseen in a century.

This year's floods in various places, at the most tense moments, people near the danger zones repeatedly recalled the dream of the flood of twenty years ago in their minds. As a result, disasters occurred, embankments collapsed, and water, compared with land in our country, is expanding on one hand and contracting on the other, creating a contradictory and incredible inverse proportion.

When water causes drought in some places, it turns the land red for thousands of miles, without a drop of sweet spring. When water causes floods in some places, boats travel on land, and huge waves roar. This kind of deformed development, the dangers, hunger, and pain suffered by the people, are like the water level markers, increasing day by day.

In the eyes of old-fashioned old women, water is only used for washing clothes, boiling tea, and cooking rice. Other than that, it has no emotional impact. Farmers, however, value water very much. If there is no water in the rice fields, they use waterwheels to irrigate them. When the rain falls and fills the banks, and the green seedlings are about to be submerged, they hope that the rain will subside. The rise and fall of the water level are closely related to the interests of the farmers. Women are made of water, and there are indeed too many fashionable women in the big cities. The production of water has become widespread and increased in recent years, creating a new record unseen in hundreds of years. According to this view, the taste of water is indeed sour, bitter, and shaking people's souls to the point of immobility. The scouring, impact, and huge waves that destroy houses are a situation that we humans are enduring. It is really unbearable!

Deliveries Primarily by Financial Institutions, with Many Retail Investors

Yesterday was the settlement date for the July futures contracts on the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange. The settlement volume did not decrease due to the change to half-day trading. The total volume was 33,395,000 yuan, an increase of 4 million yuan compared to the previous month. Among these, 22,885,000 yuan was settled through internal bookkeeping between brokers and private settlements. The actual amount settled on the exchange was 10,510,000 yuan. Although the number of off-exchange settlements by brokers is unverifiable, the quantity should not be less than 15 million. Receivers were mostly financial institutions and certain savings associations. Deliverers were mostly retail investors. Arbitrage transactions were less than the previous month. The settlement process was quite smooth, mainly due to the abundance of silver and a favorable environment. Receivers mostly benefited, and deliverers mostly suffered losses based on market prices. The overall market price trend was gradually upward, with no major fluctuations or swings. The difference between the highest and lowest prices was mostly around 12 yuan, while the difference for Positive Six (referring to a specific bond type) was over 17 yuan. Tracing back to May 27, when the July futures were first introduced, the salt tax market was at 44.45 yuan. The highest price on July 19 was 55.75 yuan. The lowest price on May 31 was 43 yuan, with a difference of 12.75 yuan between the highest and lowest prices. The highest price for Positive Six was 60 yuan, and the lowest was 42.8 yuan, with a difference of 17.2 yuan. This was because after the Ministry of Finance revised Positive Six, its treatment improved, and its total amount was only over 32 million, leading to increased demand and a price increase. Examining the trend of the process, it was indeed due to a favorable environment that led to this. The upward trend was almost a straight line. After the signing of the Sino-Japanese agreement, although there were still unfavorable news such as the insubordination of puppet troops, the difficulty of receiving North China, and the Feng army using the pretext of resisting Japan to occupy Chahar, these had little impact on the high and low market prices. Since news of the establishment of the Sino-British loan was spread, the bulls became more concentrated, and the market price directly advanced to a peak. New high prices were frequently seen. The 96 public bonds, which had long been unattended to, suddenly turned from cold to hot. On June 2, the market price was only 4.9 jiao, but it rose to as high as 21-22 yuan on July 8. Eventually, due to rumors of no interest payment and the influx of spot goods, it recently fluctuated around 8-9 yuan. The turbulence within this was relatively treacherous, and transactions were also extremely active. The total transaction volume of various July futures was 31,170,000 yuan. 96 even had 3,091 yuan, accounting for one-tenth of the total.
